<span class="akn-akomaNtoso"><article class="akn-act" data-contains="originalVersion"><span class="akn-body"><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_1" data-eId="chp_1"><h2>Chapter 1<br>General</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_1__part_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_1"><h2>Regulation 1  Application</h2>
<span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_1__term_1">Annex</span> shall apply to all ships, except where expressly provided otherwise in regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_3" href="#chp_1__part_3">3</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">6</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_13" href="#chp_3__part_13">13</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_15" href="#chp_3__part_15">15</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_16" href="#chp_3__part_16">16</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_18" href="#chp_3__part_18">18</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_19" href="#chp_4__part_19">19</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_20" href="#chp_4__part_20">20</a>, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">21</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_22" href="#chp_4__part_22">22</a> of this Annex.</span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_1__part_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2"><h2>Regulation 2  Definitions</h2>
<span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">For the purpose of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__term_1">Annex</span>:</span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Annex">Annex</span> means Annex VI to the International Convention for the Prevention of Pollution from Ships, 1973 (MARPOL), as modified by the Protocol of 1978 relating thereto, and as modified by the Protocol of 1997, as amended by the Organization, provided that such amendments are adopted and brought into force in accordance with the provisions of article 16 of the present Convention.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-A_similar_stage_of_construction"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-A_similar_stage_of_construction">A similar stage of construction</span> means the stage at which:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_2__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_2__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">construction identifiable with a specific ship begins; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_2__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_2__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">assembly of that ship has commenced comprising at least 50 tonnes or one per cent of the estimated mass of all structural material, whichever is less.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Anniversary_date"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Anniversary_date">Anniversary date</span> means the day and the month of each year that will correspond to the date of expiry of the International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_4" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Auxiliary_control_device"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Auxiliary_control_device">Auxiliary control device</span> means a system, function or control strategy <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_1__part_2__para_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_4__term_1">installed</span> on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_1__part_2__para_4__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_4__term_2">marine diesel engine</span> that is used to protect the engine and/or its ancillary equipment against operating conditions that could result in damage or failure, or that is used to facilitate the starting of the engine. An auxiliary control device may also be a strategy or measure that has been satisfactorily demonstrated not to be a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Defeat_device" id="chp_1__part_2__para_4__term_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_4__term_3">defeat device</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_5" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Continuous_feeding"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Continuous_feeding">Continuous feeding</span> is defined as the process whereby waste is fed into a combustion chamber without human assistance while the incinerator is in normal operating conditions with the combustion chamber operative temperature between 850C and 1,200C.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_6" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Defeat_device"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Defeat_device">Defeat device</span> means a device that measures, senses or responds to operating variables (e.g. engine speed, temperature, intake pressure or any other parameter) for the purpose of activating, modulating, delaying or deactivating the operation of any component or the function of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_2__para_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_6__term_1">emission</span> control system such that the effectiveness of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_2__para_6__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_6__term_2">emission</span> control system is reduced under conditions encountered during normal operation, unless the use of such a device is substantially included in the applied <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_2__para_6__term_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_6__term_3">emission</span> certification test procedures.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_7" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_7"><span class="akn-num">7</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Emission"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Emission">Emission</span> means any release of substances, subject to control by this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__para_7__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_7__term_1">Annex</span>, from ships into the atmosphere or sea.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_8" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_8"><span class="akn-num">8</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area">Emission control area</span> means an area where the adoption of special mandatory measures for emissions from ships is required to prevent, reduce and control air pollution from NO<sub>x</sub> or SOx and particulate matter or all three types of emissions and their attendant adverse impacts on human health and the environment. <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_2__para_8__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_8__term_1">Emission</span> control areas shall include those listed in, or designated under, regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_13" href="#chp_3__part_13">13</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_14" href="#chp_3__part_14">14</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_9" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_9"><span class="akn-num">9</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil">Fuel oil</span> means any fuel delivered to and intended for combustion purposes for propulsion or operation on board a ship, including gas, distillate and residual fuels.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_10" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_10"><span class="akn-num">10</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage">Gross tonnage</span> means the gross tonnage calculated in accordance with the tonnage measurement regulations contained in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__para_10__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_10__term_1">Annex</span> I to the International Convention on Tonnage Measurements of Ships, 1969, or any successor Convention.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_11" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_11"><span class="akn-num">11</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Installations in relation to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_12" href="#chp_3__part_12">regulation 12</a> of this Annex means the installation of systems, equipment, including portable fire-extinguishing units, insulation, or other material on a ship, but excludes the repair or recharge of previously installed systems, equipment, insulation or other material, or the recharge of portable fire-extinguishing units.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_12" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_12"><span class="akn-num">12</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Installed"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Installed">Installed</span> means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_1__part_2__para_12__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_12__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> that is or is intended to be fitted on a ship, including a portable auxiliary <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_1__part_2__para_12__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_12__term_2">marine diesel engine</span>, only if its fuelling, cooling or exhaust system is an integral part of the ship. A fuelling system is considered integral to the ship only if it is permanently affixed to the ship. This definition includes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_1__part_2__para_12__term_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_12__term_3">marine diesel engine</span> that is used to supplement or augment the installed power capacity of the ship and is intended to be an integral part of the ship.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_13" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_13"><span class="akn-num">13</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Irrational_emission_control_strategy"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Irrational_emission_control_strategy">Irrational emission control strategy</span> means any strategy or measure that, when the ship is operated under normal conditions of use, reduces the effectiveness of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_2__para_13__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_13__term_1">emission</span> control system to a level below that expected on the applicable <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_2__para_13__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_13__term_2">emission</span> test procedures.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_14" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_14"><span class="akn-num">14</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine">Marine diesel engine</span> means any reciprocating internal combustion engine operating on liquid or dual fuel, to which <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_13" href="#chp_3__part_13">regulation 13</a> of this Annex applies, including booster/compound systems if applied. In addition, a gas-fuelled engine installed on a ship constructed on or after 1 March 2016 or a gas-fuelled additional or non-identical replacement engine installed on or after that date is also considered as a marine diesel engine.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_15" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_15"><span class="akn-num">15</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code means the Technical Code on Control of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_2__para_15__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_15__term_1">Emission</span> of Nitrogen Oxides from Marine Diesel Engines adopted by resolution 2 of the 1997 MARPOL Conference, as amended by the Organization, provided that such amendments are adopted and brought into force in accordance with the provisions of article 16 of the present Convention.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_16" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_16"><span class="akn-num">16</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances">Ozone-depleting substances</span> means controlled substances defined in paragraph (4) of article 1 of the Montreal Protocol on Substances that Deplete the Ozone Layer, 1987, listed in Annexes A, B, C or E to the said Protocol in force at the time of application or interpretation of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__para_16__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_16__term_1">Annex</span>.</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_1__part_2__para_16__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_16__term_2">Ozone-depleting substances</span> that may be found on board ship include, but are not limited to:</span><div class="akn--table-container"><table eId="chp_1__part_2__para_16__table_1">
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Halon 1211</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Bromochlorodifluoromethane</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Halon 1301</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Bromotrifluoromethane</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Halon 2402</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">1,2-Dibromo-1,1,2,2-tetraflouroethane (also known as Halon 114B2)</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">CFC-11</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Trichlorofluoromethane</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">CFC-12</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">Dichlorodifluoromethane</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">CFC-113</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">1,1,2-Trichloro-1,2,2-trifluoroethane</span></td>

<td><span class="akn-p">CFC-114</span></td>

</table></div></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_17" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_17"><span class="akn-num">17</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incineration"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incineration">Shipboard incineration</span> means the incineration of wastes or other matter on board a ship, if such wastes or other matter were generated during the normal operation of that ship.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_18" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_18"><span class="akn-num">18</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incinerator"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incinerator">Shipboard incinerator</span> means a shipboard facility designed for the primary purpose of incineration.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_19" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_19"><span class="akn-num">19</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed">Ships constructed</span> means ships the keels of which are laid or that are at <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-A_similar_stage_of_construction" id="chp_1__part_2__para_19__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_19__term_1">a similar stage of construction</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_20" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_20"><span class="akn-num">20</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Sludge_oil"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Sludge_oil">Sludge oil</span> means sludge from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_1__part_2__para_20__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_20__term_1">fuel oil</span> or lubricating oil separators, waste lubricating oil from main or auxiliary machinery, or waste oil from bilge water separators, oil filtering equipment or drip trays.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_21" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_21"><span class="akn-num">21</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Tanker in relation to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_15" href="#chp_3__part_15">regulation 15</a> of this Annex means an oil tanker as defined in regulation 1 of Annex I of the present Convention or a chemical tanker as defined in regulation 1 of Annex II of the present Convention.</span></span></span><span class="akn-container" data-name="container" id="chp_1__part_2__container_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__container_1"><span class="akn-p">For the purpose of chapter 4:</span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_22" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_22"><span class="akn-num">22</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship">Existing ship</span> means a ship which is not a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_1__part_2__para_22__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_22__term_1">new ship</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_23" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_23"><span class="akn-num">23</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship">New ship</span> means a ship:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for which the building contract is placed on or after 1 January 2013; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">in the absence of a building contract, the keel of which is laid or which is at <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-A_similar_stage_of_construction" id="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_2__term_1">a similar stage of construction</span> on or after 1 July 2013; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_23__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the delivery of which is on or after 1 July 2015.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24"><span class="akn-num">24</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion">Major conversion</span> means in relation to chapter 4 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__term_1">Annex</span> a conversion of a ship:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">which substantially alters the dimensions, carrying capacity or engine power of the ship; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">which changes the type of the ship; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the intent of which in the opinion of the Administration is substantially to prolong the life of the ship; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">which otherwise so alters the ship that, if it were a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_4__term_1">new ship</span>, it would become subject to relevant provisions of the present Convention not applicable to it as an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_4__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_4__term_2">existing ship</span>; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_5" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_24__subpara_5"><span class="akn-num">.5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">which substantially alters the energy efficiency of the ship and includes any modifications that could cause the ship to exceed the applicable required EEDI as set out in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">regulation 21</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_25" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_25"><span class="akn-num">25</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Bulk_carrier"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Bulk_carrier">Bulk carrier</span> means a ship which is intended primarily to carry dry cargo in bulk, including such types as ore carriers as defined in regulation 1 of chapter XII of SOLAS 74 (as amended) but excluding combination carriers.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_26" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_26"><span class="akn-num">26</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Gas_carrier_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Gas_carrier_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex">Gas carrier in relation to chapter 4 of this Annex</span> means a cargo ship, other than an LNG carrier as defined in paragraph 38 of this regulation, constructed or adapted and used for the carriage in bulk of any liquefied gas.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_27" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_27"><span class="akn-num">27</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Tanker_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Tanker_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex">Tanker in relation to chapter 4 of this Annex</span> means an oil tanker as defined in regulation 1 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__para_27__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_27__term_1">Annex</span> I of the present Convention or a chemical tanker or an NLS tanker as defined in regulation 1 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__para_27__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_27__term_2">Annex</span> II of the present Convention.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_28" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_28"><span class="akn-num">28</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Containership"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Containership">Containership</span> means a ship designed exclusively for the carriage of containers in holds and on deck.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_29" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_29"><span class="akn-num">29</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-General_cargo_ship"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-General_cargo_ship">General cargo ship</span> means a ship with a multi-deck or single deck hull designed primarily for the carriage of general cargo. This definition excludes specialized dry cargo ships, which are not included in the calculation of reference lines for general cargo ships, namely livestock carrier, barge carrier, heavy load carrier, yacht carrier, nuclear fuel carrier.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_30" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_30"><span class="akn-num">30</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Refrigerated_cargo_carrier"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Refrigerated_cargo_carrier">Refrigerated cargo carrier</span> means a ship designed exclusively for the carriage of refrigerated cargoes in holds.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_31" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_31"><span class="akn-num">31</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Combination_carrier"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Combination_carrier">Combination carrier</span> means a ship designed to load 100% deadweight with both liquid and dry cargo in bulk.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_32" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_32"><span class="akn-num">32</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Passenger_ship"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Passenger_ship">Passenger ship</span> means a ship which carries more than 12 passengers.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_33" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_33"><span class="akn-num">33</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Ro_ro_cargo_ship__vehicle_carrier_"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Ro_ro_cargo_ship__vehicle_carrier_"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ro_ro_cargo_ship" id="chp_1__part_2__para_33__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_33__term_1">Ro-ro cargo ship</span> (vehicle carrier)</span> means a multi deck roll-on-roll-off cargo ship designed for the carriage of empty cars and trucks.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_34" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_34"><span class="akn-num">34</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Ro_ro_cargo_ship"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Ro_ro_cargo_ship">Ro-ro cargo ship</span> means a ship designed for the carriage of roll-on-roll-off cargo transportation units.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_35" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_35"><span class="akn-num">35</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Ro_ro_passenger_ship"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Ro_ro_passenger_ship">Ro-ro passenger ship</span> means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Passenger_ship" id="chp_1__part_2__para_35__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_35__term_1">passenger ship</span> with roll-on-roll-off cargo spaces.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_36" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_36"><span class="akn-num">36</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Attained EEDI is the EEDI value achieved by an individual ship in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_20" href="#chp_4__part_20">regulation 20</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_37" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_37"><span class="akn-num">37</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Required EEDI is the maximum value of attained EEDI that is allowed by <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">regulation 21</a> of this Annex for the specific ship type and size.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_38" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_38"><span class="akn-num">38</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-LNG_carrier_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-LNG_carrier_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex">LNG carrier in relation to chapter 4 of this Annex</span> means a cargo ship constructed or adapted and used for the carriage in bulk of liquefied natural gas (LNG).</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_39" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_39"><span class="akn-num">39</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Cruise_passenger_ship_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Cruise_passenger_ship_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex">Cruise passenger ship in relation to chapter 4 of this Annex</span> means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Passenger_ship" id="chp_1__part_2__para_39__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_39__term_1">passenger ship</span> not having a cargo deck, designed exclusively for commercial transportation of passengers in overnight accommodations on a sea voyage.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_40" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_40"><span class="akn-num">40</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Conventional_propulsion_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Conventional_propulsion_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex">Conventional propulsion in relation to chapter 4 of this Annex</span> means a method of propulsion where a main reciprocating internal combustion engine(s) is the prime mover and coupled to a propulsion shaft either directly or through a gear box.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_41" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_41"><span class="akn-num">41</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Non_conventional_propulsion_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Non_conventional_propulsion_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex">Non-conventional propulsion in relation to chapter 4 of this Annex</span> means a method of propulsion, other than conventional propulsion, including diesel-electric propulsion, turbine propulsion, and hybrid propulsion systems.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_42" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_42"><span class="akn-num">42</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Cargo_ship_having_ice_breaking_capability_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Cargo_ship_having_ice_breaking_capability_in_relation_to_chapter_4_of_this_Annex">Cargo ship having ice-breaking capability in relation to chapter 4 of this Annex</span> means a cargo ship which is designed to break level ice independently with a speed of at least 2 knots when the level ice thickness is 1.0 m or more having ice bending strength of at least 500 kPa.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_43" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_43"><span class="akn-num">43</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-A_ship_delivered_on_or_after_1_September_2019"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-A_ship_delivered_on_or_after_1_September_2019">A ship delivered on or after 1 September 2019</span> means a ship:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for which the building contract is placed on or after 1 September 2015; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">in the absence of a building contract, the keel of which is laid, or which is at <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-A_similar_stage_of_construction" id="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_3__term_1">a similar stage of construction</span>, on or after 1 March 2016; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_43__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the delivery of which is on or after 1 September 2019.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-container" data-name="container" id="chp_1__part_2__container_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__container_2"><span class="akn-p">For the purposes of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_2__container_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__container_2__term_1">Annex</span>:</span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_44" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_44"><span class="akn-num">44</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Audit"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Audit">Audit</span> means a systematic, independent and documented process for obtaining audit evidence and evaluating it objectively to determine the extent to which audit criteria are fulfilled.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_45" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_45"><span class="akn-num">45</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Scheme"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Scheme">Audit Scheme</span> means the IMO Member State Audit Scheme established by the Organization and taking into account the guidelines developed by the Organization<sup><a href="#chp_1__part_2__para_45__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_1__part_2__para_45__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_45__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to the Framework and Procedures for the IMO Member State Audit Scheme (resolution A.1067(28)).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_46" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_46"><span class="akn-num">46</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Code_for_Implementation"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Code_for_Implementation">Code for Implementation</span> means the IMO Instruments Implementation Code (III Code) adopted by the Organization by resolution A.1070(28).</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_2__para_47" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_47"><span class="akn-num">47</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Standard"><span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Standard">Audit Standard</span> means the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Code_for_Implementation" id="chp_1__part_2__para_47__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_2__para_47__term_1">Code for Implementation</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_1__part_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_3"><h2>Regulation 3  Exceptions and exemptions</h2>
<div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_1"><h3 id="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_1">General</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Regulations of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__term_1">Annex</span> shall not apply to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_1__term_1">emission</span> necessary for the purpose of securing the safety of a ship or saving life at sea; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__term_1">emission</span> resulting from damage to a ship or its equipment:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21"><span class="akn-num">2.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">provided that all reasonable precautions have been taken after the occurrence of the damage or discovery of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21__term_1">emission</span> for the purpose of preventing or minimizing the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21__term_2">emission</span>; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_1__subpara_2__subpara_21"><span class="akn-num">2.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">except if the owner or the master acted either with intent to cause damage, or recklessly and with knowledge that damage would probably result.</span></span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_2"><h3 id="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_2">Trials for ship <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_2__term_1">emission</span> reduction and control technology research</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">The Administration of a Party may, in cooperation with other Administrations as appropriate, issue an exemption from specific provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_3__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_2__term_1">Annex</span> for a ship to conduct trials for the development of ship <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_1__part_3__para_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_2__term_2">emission</span> reduction and control technologies and engine design programmes. Such an exemption shall only be provided if the applications of specific provisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_3__para_2__term_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_2__term_3">Annex</span> or the revised NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code 2008 could impede research into the development of such technologies or programmes. A permit for such an exemption shall only be provided to the minimum number of ships necessary and be subject to the following provisions:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_2__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_2__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for marine diesel engines with a per cylinder displacement up to 30 L, the duration of the sea trial shall not exceed 18 months. If additional time is required, a permitting Administration or Administrations may permit a renewal for one additional 18-month period; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_2__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_2__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for marine diesel engines with a per cylinder displacement at or above 30 L, the duration of the ship trial shall not exceed five years and shall require a progress review by the permitting Administration or Administrations at each intermediate survey. A permit may be withdrawn based on this review if the testing has not adhered to the conditions of the permit or if it is determined that the technology or programme is not likely to produce effective results in the reduction and control of ship emissions. If the reviewing Administration or Administrations determine that additional time is required to conduct a test of a particular technology or programme, a permit may be renewed for an additional time period not to exceed five years.</span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_3"><h3 id="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__crossHeading_3">Emissions from sea-bed mineral activities</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_31" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_31"><span class="akn-num">3.1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Emissions directly arising from the exploration, exploitation and associated offshore processing of sea-bed mineral resources are, consistent with article 2(3)(b)(ii) of the present Convention, exempt from the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_3__para_31__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_31__term_1">Annex</span>. Such emissions include the following:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">emissions resulting from the incineration of substances that are solely and directly the result of exploration, exploitation and associated offshore processing of sea-bed mineral resources, including but not limited to the flaring of hydrocarbons and the burning of cuttings, muds, and/or stimulation fluids during well completion and testing operations, and flaring arising from upset conditions;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the release of gases and volatile compounds entrained in drilling fluids and cuttings;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">emissions associated solely and directly with the treatment, handling or storage of sea-bed minerals; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_31__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">emissions from marine diesel engines that are solely dedicated to the exploration, exploitation and associated offshore processing of sea-bed mineral resources.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_3__para_32" data-eId="chp_1__part_3__para_32"><span class="akn-num">3.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The requirements of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_18" href="#chp_3__part_18">regulation 18</a> of this Annex shall not apply to the use of hydrocarbons that are produced and subsequently used on site as fuel, when approved by the Administration.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_1__part_4" data-eId="chp_1__part_4"><h2>Regulation 4  Equivalents</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_4__para_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_4__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration of a Party may allow any fitting, material, appliance or apparatus to be fitted in a ship or other procedures, alternative fuel oils, or compliance methods used as an alternative to that required by this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_4__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_4__para_1__term_1">Annex</span> if such fitting, material, appliance or apparatus or other procedures, alternative fuel oils, or compliance methods are at least as effective in terms of emissions reductions as that required by this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_4__para_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_4__para_1__term_2">Annex</span>, including any of the standards set forth in regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_13" href="#chp_3__part_13">13</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_14" href="#chp_3__part_14">14</a>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_4__para_2" data-eId="chp_1__part_4__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration of a Party that allows a fitting, material, appliance or apparatus or other procedures, alternative fuel oils, or compliance methods used as an alternative to that required by this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_1__part_4__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__part_4__para_2__term_1">Annex</span> shall communicate to the Organization for circulation to the Parties particulars thereof, for their information and appropriate action, if any.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_4__para_3" data-eId="chp_1__part_4__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration of a Party should take into account any relevant guidelines developed by the Organization[3] pertaining to the equivalents provided for in this regulation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_1__part_4__para_4" data-eId="chp_1__part_4__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration of a Party that allows the use of an equivalent as set forth in paragraph 1 of this regulation shall endeavour not to impair or damage its environment, human health, property or resources or those of other States.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_2" data-eId="chp_2"><h2>Chapter 2<br>Survey, certification and means of control</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_5" data-eId="chp_2__part_5"><h2>Regulation 5  Surveys</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Every ship of 400 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__term_1">gross tonnage</span> and above and every fixed and floating drilling rig and other platforms shall, to ensure compliance with the requirements of chapter 3 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__term_2">Annex</span>, be subject to the surveys specified below:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An initial survey before the ship is put into service or before the certificate required under <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">regulation 6</a> of this Annex is issued for the first time. This survey shall be such as to ensure that the equipment, systems, fittings, arrangements and material fully comply with the applicable requirements of chapter 3 of this Annex;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A renewal survey at intervals specified by the Administration, but not exceeding five years, except where regulation <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_9" href="#chp_2__part_9">9</a>.2, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_9" href="#chp_2__part_9">9</a>.5, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_9" href="#chp_2__part_9">9</a>.6 or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_9" href="#chp_2__part_9">9</a>.7 of this Annex is applicable. The renewal survey shall be such as to ensure that the equipment, systems, fittings, arrangements and material fully comply with applicable requirements of chapter 3 of this Annex;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An intermediate survey within three months before or after the second <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Anniversary_date" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3__term_1">anniversary date</span> or within three months before or after the third <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Anniversary_date" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3__term_2">anniversary date</span> of the certificate which shall take the place of one of the annual surveys specified in paragraph 1.4 of this regulation. The intermediate survey shall be such as to ensure that the equipment and arrangements fully comply with the applicable requirements of chapter 3 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3__term_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_3__term_3">Annex</span> and are in good working order. Such intermediate surveys shall be endorsed on the IAPP Certificate issued under regulation <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">6</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_7" href="#chp_2__part_7">7</a> of this Annex;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An annual survey within three months before or after each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Anniversary_date" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_4__term_1">anniversary date</span> of the certificate, including a general inspection of the equipment, systems, fittings, arrangements and material referred to in paragraph 1.1 of this regulation to ensure that they have been maintained in accordance with paragraph 5 of this regulation and that they remain satisfactory for the service for which the ship is intended. Such annual surveys shall be endorsed on the IAPP Certificate issued under regulation <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">6</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_7" href="#chp_2__part_7">7</a> of this Annex; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_5" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_5"><span class="akn-num">.5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An additional survey either general or partial, according to the circumstances, shall be made whenever any important repairs or renewals are made as prescribed in paragraph 5 of this regulation or after a repair resulting from investigations prescribed in paragraph 6 of this regulation. The survey shall be such as to ensure that the necessary repairs or renewals have been effectively made, that the material and workmanship of such repairs or renewals are in all respects satisfactory and that the ship complies in all respects with the requirements of chapter 3 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_1__subpara_5__term_1">Annex</span>.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the case of ships of less than 400 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_2__part_5__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_2__term_1">gross tonnage</span>, the Administration may establish appropriate measures in order to ensure that the applicable provisions of chapter 3 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_2__term_2">Annex</span> are complied with.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Surveys of ships as regards the enforcement of the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3__term_1">Annex</span> shall be carried out by officers of the Administration.</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration may, however, entrust the surveys either to surveyors nominated for the purpose or to organizations recognized by it. Such organizations shall comply with the guidelines adopted by the Organization;<sup><a href="#chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_1__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_1__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_1__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Guidelines for the authorization of organizations acting on behalf of the Administration (resolution A.739(18), as amended by resolution MSC.208(81)), and Specifications on the survey and certification functions of recognized organizations acting on behalf of the Administration (resolution A.789(19), as may be amended). Refer also to Survey Guidelines under the Harmonized System of Survey and Certification for the revised MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_1__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_1__authorialNote_1__term_1">Annex</span> VI (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.180%2859%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.180%2859%29.pdf">MEPC.180(59)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The survey of marine diesel engines and equipment for compliance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_13" href="#chp_3__part_13">regulation 13</a> of this Annex shall be conducted in accordance with the revised NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code 2008;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When a nominated surveyor or recognized organization determines that the condition of the equipment does not correspond substantially with the particulars of the certificate, it shall ensure that corrective action is taken and shall in due course notify the Administration. If such corrective action is not taken, the certificate shall be withdrawn by the Administration. If the ship is in a port of another Party, the appropriate authorities of the port State shall also be notified immediately. When an officer of the Administration, a nominated surveyor or recognized organization has notified the appropriate authorities of the port State, the Government of the port State concerned shall give such officer, surveyor or organization any necessary assistance to carry out their obligations under this regulation; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_3__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In every case, thme Administration concerned shall fully guarantee the completeness and efficiency of the survey and shall undertake to ensure the necessary arrangements to satisfy this obligation.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Ships to which chapter 4 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__term_1">Annex</span> applies shall also be subject to the surveys specified below, taking into account the guidelines adopted by the Organization:<sup><a href="#chp_2__part_5__para_4__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2014 Guidelines on survey and certification of the Energy Efficiency Design Index (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.254%2867%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.254%2867%29.pdf">MEPC.254(67)</a>, as amended by resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.261%2868%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.261%2868%29.pdf">MEPC.261(68)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An initial survey before a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_1__term_1">new ship</span> is put in service and before the International Energy Efficiency Certificate is issued. The survey shall verify that the ships attained EEDI is in accordance with the requirements in chapter 4 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_1__term_2">Annex</span>, and that the SEEMP required by <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_22" href="#chp_4__part_22">regulation 22</a> of this Annex is on board;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A general or partial survey, according to the circumstances, after a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_2__term_1">major conversion</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_2__term_2">new ship</span> to which this regulation applies. The survey shall ensure that the attained EEDI is recalculated as necessary and meets the requirement of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">regulation 21</a> of this Annex, with the reduction factor applicable to the ship type and size of the converted ship in the phase corresponding to the date of contract or keel laying or delivery determined for the original ship in accordance with <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">regulation 2</a>.23 of this Annex;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In cases where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_3__term_1">major conversion</span> of a new or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_3__term_2">existing ship</span> is so extensive that the ship is regarded by the Administration as a newly constructed ship, the Administration shall determine the necessity of an initial survey on attained EEDI. Such a survey, if determined necessary, shall ensure that the attained EEDI is calculated and meets the requirement of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">regulation 21</a> of this Annex, with the reduction factor applicable corresponding to the ship type and size of the converted ship at the date of the contract of the conversion, or in the absence of a contract, the commencement date of the conversion. The survey shall also verify that the SEEMP required by <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_22" href="#chp_4__part_22">regulation 22</a> of this Annex is on board; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_4__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For existing ships, the verification of the requirement to have a SEEMP on board according to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_22" href="#chp_4__part_22">regulation 22</a> of this Annex shall take place at the first intermediate or renewal survey identified in paragraph 1 of this regulation, whichever is the first, on or after 1 January 2013.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_5" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The equipment shall be maintained to conform with the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_5__term_1">Annex</span> and no changes shall be made in the equipment, systems, fittings, arrangements or material covered by the survey, without the express approval of the Administration. The direct replacement of such equipment and fittings with equipment and fittings that conform with the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_5__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_5__term_2">Annex</span> is permitted.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_5__para_6" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Whenever an accident occurs to a ship or a defect is discovered that substantially affects the efficiency or completeness of its equipment covered by this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_5__para_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_5__para_6__term_1">Annex</span>, the master or owner of the ship shall report at the earliest opportunity to the Administration, a nominated surveyor or recognized organization responsible for issuing the relevant certificate.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_6" data-eId="chp_2__part_6"><h2>Regulation 6  Issue or endorsement of Certificates</h2>
<div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_1"><h3 id="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_1">International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_6__para_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">An International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate shall be issued, after an initial or renewal survey in accordance with the provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">regulation 5</a> of this Annex, to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_6__para_1__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_1__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">any ship of 400 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_2__part_6__para_1__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_1__subpara_1__term_1">gross tonnage</span> and above engaged in voyages to ports or offshore terminals under the jurisdiction of other Parties; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_6__para_1__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_1__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">platforms and drilling rigs engaged in voyages to waters under the sovereignty or jurisdiction of other Parties.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_6__para_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A ship constructed before the date this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_6__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_2__term_1">Annex</span> enters into force for that particular ships Administration, shall be issued with an International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate in accordance with paragraph 1 of this regulation no later than the first scheduled dry-docking after the date of such entry into force, but in no case later than three years after this date.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_6__para_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Such certificate shall be issued or endorsed either by the Administration or by any person or organization duly authorized by it.[6] In every case, the Administration assumes full responsibility for the certificate.</span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_2"><h3 id="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__crossHeading_2">International Energy Efficiency Certificate</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_6__para_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An International Energy Efficiency Certificate for the ship shall be issued after a survey in accordance with the provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">regulation 5</a>.4 of this Annex to any ship of 400 gross tonnage and above before that ship may engage in voyages to ports or offshore terminals under the jurisdiction of other Parties.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_6__para_5" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The certificate shall be issued or endorsed either by the Administration or any organization duly authorized by it.<sup><a href="#chp_2__part_6__para_5__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup> In every case, the Administration assumes full responsibility for the certificate.<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_2__part_6__para_5__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_6__para_5__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Guidelines for the authorization of organizations acting on behalf of the Administration (resolution A.739(18), as amended by resolution MSC.208(81)), and Specifications on the survey and certification functions of recognized organizations acting on behalf of the Administration (resolution A.789(19), as may be amended).</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_7" data-eId="chp_2__part_7"><h2>Regulation 7  Issue of a Certificate by another Party</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_7__para_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_7__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A Party may, at the request of the Administration, cause a ship to be surveyed and, if satisfied that the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_7__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_7__para_1__term_1">Annex</span> are complied with, shall issue or authorize the issuance of an International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate or an International Energy Efficiency Certificate to the ship, and where appropriate, endorse or authorize the endorsement of such certificates on the ship, in accordance with this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_7__para_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_7__para_1__term_2">Annex</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_7__para_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_7__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A copy of the certificate and a copy of the survey report shall be transmitted as soon as possible to the requesting Administration.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_7__para_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_7__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A certificate so issued shall contain a statement to the effect that it has been issued at the request of the Administration and it shall have the same force and receive the same recognition as a certificate issued under <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">regulation 6</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_7__para_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_7__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate or an International Energy Efficiency Certificate shall be issued to a ship which is entitled to fly the flag of a State which is not a Party.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_8" data-eId="chp_2__part_8"><h2>Regulation 8  Form of Certificates</h2>
<div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_1"><h3 id="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_1">International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_8__para_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The International Air Pollution Prevention (IAPP) Certificate shall be drawn up in a form corresponding to the model given in appendix I to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_8__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__para_1__term_1">Annex</span> and shall be at least in English, French or Spanish. If an official language of the issuing country is also used, this shall prevail in case of a dispute or discrepancy.</span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_2"><h3 id="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__crossHeading_2">International Energy Efficiency Certificate</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_8__para_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The International Energy Efficiency Certificate shall be drawn up in a form corresponding to the model given in appendix VIII to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_8__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_8__para_2__term_1">Annex</span> and shall be at least in English, French or Spanish. If an official language of the issuing Party is also used, this shall prevail in case of a dispute or discrepancy.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_9" data-eId="chp_2__part_9"><h2>Regulation 9  Duration and validity of Certificates</h2>
<div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_1"><h3 id="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_1">International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An International Air Pollution Prevention (IAPP) Certificate shall be issued for a period specified by the Administration, which shall not exceed five years.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the requirements of paragraph 1 of this regulation:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_2__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_2__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">when the renewal survey is completed within three months before the expiry date of the existing certificate, the new certificate shall be valid from the date of completion of the renewal survey to a date not exceeding five years from the date of expiry of the existing certificate;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_2__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_2__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">when the renewal survey is completed after the expiry date of the existing certificate, the new certificate shall be valid from the date of completion of the renewal survey to a date not exceeding five years from the date of expiry of the existing certificate; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_2__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_2__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">when the renewal survey is completed more than three months before the expiry date of the existing certificate, the new certificate shall be valid from the date of completion of the renewal survey to a date not exceeding five years from the date of completion of the renewal survey.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a certificate is issued for a period of less than five years, the Administration may extend the validity of the certificate beyond the expiry date to the maximum period specified in paragraph 1 of this regulation, provided that the surveys referred to in regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a>.1.3 and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a>.1.4 of this Annex applicable when a certificate is issued for a period of five years are carried out as appropriate.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a renewal survey has been completed and a new certificate cannot be issued or placed on board the ship before the expiry date of the existing certificate, the person or organization authorized by the Administration may endorse the existing certificate and such a certificate shall be accepted as valid for a further period that shall not exceed five months from the expiry date.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_5" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a ship, at the time when a certificate expires, is not in a port in which it is to be surveyed, the Administration may extend the period of validity of the certificate, but this extension shall be granted only for the purpose of allowing the ship to complete its voyage to the port in which it is to be surveyed, and then only in cases where it appears proper and reasonable to do so. No certificate shall be extended for a period longer than three months, and a ship to which an extension is granted shall not, on its arrival in the port in which it is to be surveyed, be entitled by virtue of such extension to leave that port without having a new certificate. When the renewal survey is completed, the new certificate shall be valid to a date not exceeding five years from the date of expiry of the existing certificate before the extension was granted.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_6" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A certificate issued to a ship engaged on short voyages that has not been extended under the foregoing provisions of this regulation may be extended by the Administration for a period of grace of up to one month from the date of expiry stated on it.
