When the renewal survey is completed, the new certificate shall be valid to a date not exceeding five years from the date of expiry of the existing certificate before the extension was granted.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_7" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_7"><span class="akn-num">7</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In special circumstances, as determined by the Administration, a new certificate need not be dated from the date of expiry of the existing certificate as required by paragraph 2.1, 5 or 6 of this regulation. In these special circumstances, the new certificate shall be valid to a date not exceeding five years from the date of completion of the renewal survey.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_8" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_8"><span class="akn-num">8</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">If an annual or intermediate survey is completed before the period specified in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">regulation 5</a> of this Annex, then:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Anniversary_date" id="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_1__term_1">anniversary date</span> shown on the certificate shall be amended by endorsement to a date that shall not be more than three months later than the date on which the survey was completed;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the subsequent annual or intermediate survey required by <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">regulation 5</a> of this Annex shall be completed at the intervals prescribed by that regulation using the new anniversary date; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_8__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the expiry date may remain unchanged, provided one or more annual or intermediate surveys, as appropriate, are carried out so that the maximum intervals between the surveys prescribed by <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">regulation 5</a> of this Annex are not exceeded.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_9" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_9"><span class="akn-num">9</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">A certificate issued under regulation <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">6</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_7" href="#chp_2__part_7">7</a> of this Annex shall cease to be valid in any of the following cases:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_9__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_9__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">if the relevant surveys are not completed within the periods specified under <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">regulation 5</a>.1 of this Annex;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_9__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_9__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">if the certificate is not endorsed in accordance with regulation <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a>.1.3 or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a>.1.4 of this Annex; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_9__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_9__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">upon transfer of the ship to the flag of another State. A new certificate shall only be issued when the Government issuing the new certificate is fully satisfied that the ship is in compliance with the requirements of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">regulation 5</a>.4 of this Annex. In the case of a transfer between Parties, if requested within three months after the transfer has taken place, the Government of the Party whose flag the ship was formerly entitled to fly shall, as soon as possible, transmit to the Administration copies of the certificate carried by the ship before the transfer and, if available, copies of the relevant survey reports.</span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_2"><h3 id="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__crossHeading_2">International Energy Efficiency Certificate</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_10" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_10"><span class="akn-num">10</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The International Energy Efficiency Certificate shall be valid throughout the life of the ship subject to the provisions of paragraph 11 below.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_11" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_11"><span class="akn-num">11</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">An International Energy Efficiency Certificate issued under this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_9__para_11__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_11__term_1">Annex</span> shall cease to be valid in any of the following cases:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">if the ship is withdrawn from service or if a new certificate is issued following <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_1__term_1">major conversion</span> of the ship; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">upon transfer of the ship to the flag of another State. A new certificate shall only be issued when the Government issuing the new certificate is fully satisfied that the ship is in compliance with the requirements of chapter 4 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_9__para_11__subpara_2__term_1">Annex</span>. In the case of a transfer between Parties, if requested within three months after the transfer has taken place, the Government of the Party whose flag the ship was formerly entitled to fly shall, as soon as possible, transmit to the Administration copies of the certificate carried by the ship before the transfer and, if available, copies of the relevant survey reports.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_10" data-eId="chp_2__part_10"><h2>Regulation 10  Port State control on operational requirements</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_10__para_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A ship, when in a port or an offshore terminal under the jurisdiction of another Party, is subject to inspection by officers duly authorized by such Party concerning operational requirements under this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_10__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_1__term_1">Annex</span>,<sup><a href="#chp_2__part_10__para_1__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup> where there are clear grounds for believing that the master or crew are not familiar with essential shipboard procedures relating to the prevention of air pollution from ships.<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_2__part_10__para_1__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_1__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Procedures for port State control (resolution A.1052(27)). Refer also to 2009 Guidelines for port State control under the revised MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_10__para_1__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_1__authorialNote_1__term_1">Annex</span> VI (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.181%2859%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.181%2859%29.pdf">MEPC.181(59)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_10__para_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the circumstances given in paragraph 1 of this regulation, the Party shall take such steps as to ensure that the ship shall not sail until the situation has been brought to order in accordance with the requirements of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_10__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_2__term_1">Annex</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_10__para_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Procedures relating to the port State control prescribed in article 5 of the present Convention shall apply to this regulation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_10__para_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Nothing in this regulation shall be construed to limit the rights and obligations of a Party carrying out control over operational requirements specifically provided for in the present Convention.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_10__para_5" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In relation to chapter 4 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_10__para_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_10__para_5__term_1">Annex</span>, any port State inspection shall be limited to verifying, when appropriate, that there is a valid International Energy Efficiency Certificate on board, in accordance with article 5 of the Convention.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_11" data-eId="chp_2__part_11"><h2>Regulation 11  Detection of violations and enforcement</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_11__para_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Parties shall cooperate in the detection of violations and the enforcement of the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_1__term_1">Annex</span>, using all appropriate and practicable measures of detection and environmental monitoring, adequate procedures for reporting and accumulation of evidence.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_11__para_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A ship to which this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_1">Annex</span> applies may, in any port or offshore terminal of a Party, be subject to inspection by officers appointed or authorized by that Party for the purpose of verifying whether the ship has emitted any of the substances covered by this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_2">Annex</span> in violation of the provision of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_3">Annex</span>. If an inspection indicates a violation of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_2__term_4">Annex</span>, a report shall be forwarded to the Administration for any appropriate action.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_11__para_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any Party shall furnish to the Administration evidence, if any, that the ship has emitted any of the substances covered by this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_3__term_1">Annex</span> in violation of the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_3__term_2">Annex</span>. If it is practicable to do so, the competent authority of the former Party shall notify the master of the ship of the alleged violation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_11__para_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Upon receiving such evidence, the Administration so informed shall investigate the matter, and may request the other Party to furnish further or better evidence of the alleged contravention. If the Administration is satisfied that sufficient evidence is available to enable proceedings to be brought in respect of the alleged violation, it shall cause such proceedings to be taken in accordance with its law as soon as possible. The Administration shall promptly inform the Party that has reported the alleged violation, as well as the Organization, of the action taken.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_11__para_5" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A Party may also inspect a ship to which this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_5__term_1">Annex</span> applies when it enters the ports or offshore terminals under its jurisdiction, if a request for an investigation is received from any Party together with sufficient evidence that the ship has emitted any of the substances covered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_5__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_5__term_2">Annex</span> in any place in violation of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_5__term_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_5__term_3">Annex</span>. The report of such investigation shall be sent to the Party requesting it and to the Administration so that the appropriate action may be taken under the present Convention.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_2__part_11__para_6" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The international law concerning the prevention, reduction and control of pollution of the marine environment from ships, including that law relating to enforcement and safeguards, in force at the time of application or interpretation of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_6__term_1">Annex</span>, applies, mutatis mutandis, to the rules and standards set forth in this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_2__part_11__para_6__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_11__para_6__term_2">Annex</span>.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_3" data-eId="chp_3"><h2>Chapter 3<br>Requirements for control of emissions from ships</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_12" data-eId="chp_3__part_12"><h2>Regulation 12  <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__term_1">Ozone-depleting substances</span>
</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This regulation does not apply to permanently sealed equipment where there are no refrigerant charging connections or potentially removable components containing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_1__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to the provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_3" href="#chp_1__part_3">regulation 3</a>.1, any deliberate emissions of ozone-depleting substances shall be prohibited. Deliberate emissions include emissions occurring in the course of maintaining, servicing, repairing or disposing of systems or equipment, except that deliberate emissions do not include minimal releases associated with the recapture or recycling of an ozone-depleting substance. Emissions arising from leaks of an ozone-depleting substance, whether or not the leaks are deliberate, may be regulated by Parties.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_31" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_31"><span class="akn-num">3.1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Installations that contain <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_31__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_31__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span>, other than hydrochlorofluorocarbons, shall be prohibited:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed" id="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_1__term_1">ships constructed</span> on or after 19 May 2005; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">in the case of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed" id="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_31__subpara_2__term_1">ships constructed</span> before 19 May 2005, which have a contractual delivery date of the equipment to the ship on or after 19 May 2005 or, in the absence of a contractual delivery date, the actual delivery of the equipment to the ship on or after 19 May 2005.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_32" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_32"><span class="akn-num">3.2.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Installations that contain hydrochlorofluorocarbons shall be prohibited:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed" id="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_1__term_1">ships constructed</span> on or after 1 January 2020; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">in the case of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed" id="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_32__subpara_2__term_1">ships constructed</span> before 1 January 2020, which have a contractual delivery date of the equipment to the ship on or after 1 January 2020 or, in the absence of a contractual delivery date, the actual delivery of the equipment to the ship on or after 1 January 2020.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The substances referred to in this regulation, and equipment containing such substances, shall be delivered to appropriate reception facilities when removed from ships.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each ship subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">regulation 6</a>.1 shall maintain a list of equipment containing ozone-depleting substances.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_12__para_5__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_12__para_5__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_5__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">See appendix I, Supplement to International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate (IAPP Certificate), section 2.1.</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each ship subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">regulation 6</a>.1 that has rechargeable systems that contain ozone-depleting substances shall maintain an ozone-depleting substances record book. This record book may form part of an existing logbook or electronic recording system as approved by the Administration.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7"><span class="akn-num">7</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Entries in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span> record book shall be recorded in terms of mass (kg) of substance and shall be completed without delay on each occasion, in respect of the following:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">recharge, full or partial, of equipment containing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_1__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">repair or maintenance of equipment containing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_2__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">discharge of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span> to the atmosphere:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3__subpara_31" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3__subpara_31"><span class="akn-num">3.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">deliberate; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3__subpara_32" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_3__subpara_32"><span class="akn-num">3.2.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">non-deliberate;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">discharge of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_4__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span> to land-based reception facilities; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_5"><span class="akn-num">.5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">supply of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_12__para_7__subpara_5__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span> to the ship.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_13" data-eId="chp_3__part_13"><h2>Regulation 13  Nitrogen oxides (NO<sub>x</sub>)</h2>
<div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_1"><h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_1">Application</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_11" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_11"><span class="akn-num">1.1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">This regulation shall apply to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_1__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> with a power output of more than 130 kW <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_1__term_2">installed</span> on a ship; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_2__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> with a power output of more than 130 kW that undergoes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_11__subpara_2__term_2">major conversion</span> on or after 1 January 2000 except when demonstrated to the satisfaction of the Administration that such engine is an identical replacement to the engine that it is replacing and is otherwise not covered under paragraph 1.1.1 of this regulation.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12"><span class="akn-num">1.2.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">This regulation does not apply to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> intended to be used solely for emergencies, or solely to power any device or equipment intended to be used solely for emergencies on the ship on which it is <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_2">installed</span>, or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_3">marine diesel engine</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_1__term_4">installed</span> in lifeboats intended to be used solely for emergencies; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_2__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_12__subpara_2__term_2">installed</span> on a ship solely engaged in voyages within waters subject to the sovereignty or jurisdiction of the State the flag of which the ship is entitled to fly, provided that such engine is subject to an alternative NO<sub>x</sub> control measure established by the Administration.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_13" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_13"><span class="akn-num">1.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph 1.1 of this regulation, the Administration may provide an exclusion from the application of this regulation for any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> that is <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_2">installed</span> on a ship constructed, or for any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_3">marine diesel engine</span> that undergoes a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_4">major conversion</span>, before 19 May 2005, provided that the ship on which the engine is <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_13__term_5">installed</span> is solely engaged in voyages to ports or offshore terminals within the State the flag of which the ship is entitled to fly.</span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_2"><h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_2"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_2__term_1">Major conversion</span></h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21"><span class="akn-num">2.1.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">For the purpose of this regulation, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__term_1">major conversion</span> means a modification on or after 1 January 2000 of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__term_2">marine diesel engine</span> that has not already been certified to the standards set forth in paragraph 3, 4, or 5.1.1 of this regulation where:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the engine is replaced by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> or an additional <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1__term_2">marine diesel engine</span> is <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_1__term_3">installed</span>, or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">any substantial modification, as defined in the revised NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code 2008, is made to the engine, or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_21__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the maximum continuous rating of the engine is increased by more than 10% compared to the maximum continuous rating of the original certification of the engine.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_22" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_22"><span class="akn-num">2.2.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_1">major conversion</span> involving the replacement of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_2">marine diesel engine</span> with a non-identical <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_3">marine diesel engine</span>, or the installation of an additional <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_22__term_4">marine diesel engine</span>, the standards in this regulation at the time of the replacement or addition of the engine shall apply. In the case of replacement engines only, if it is not possible for such a replacement engine to meet the standards set forth in paragraph 5.1.1 of this regulation (Tier III, as applicable), then that replacement engine shall meet the standards set forth in paragraph 4 of this regulation (Tier II), taking into account guidelines developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_13__para_22__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_13__para_22__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_22__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2013 Guidelines as required by regulation 13.2.2 of MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_22__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_22__authorialNote_1__term_1">Annex</span> VI in respect of non-identical replacement engines not required to meet the Tier III limit (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.230%2865%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.230%2865%29.pdf">MEPC.230(65)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_23" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_23"><span class="akn-num">2.3.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_23__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_23__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> referred to in paragraph 2.1.2 or 2.1.3 of this regulation shall meet the following standards:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_1__term_1">ships constructed</span> prior to 1 January 2000, the standards set forth in paragraph 3 of this regulation shall apply; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ships_constructed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_23__subpara_2__term_1">ships constructed</span> on or after 1 January 2000, the standards in force at the time the ship was constructed shall apply.</span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_3">
<h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_3">Tier I<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup>
</h3>
<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Guidelines for the application of the NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code relative to certification and amendments of Tier I engines (MEPC.1/Circ.679).</span></span></span>
</div>
<span class="akn-container" data-name="container" id="chp_3__part_13__container_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__container_1"></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_3" href="#chp_1__part_3">regulation 3</a> of this Annex, the operation of a marine diesel engine that is installed on a ship constructed on or after 1 January 2000 and prior to 1 January 2011 is prohibited, except when the emission of nitrogen oxides (calculated as the total weighted emission of NO2) from the engine is within the following limits, where <i>n</i> = rated engine speed (crankshaft revolutions per minute):</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_3__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_3__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">17.0 g/kWh when n is less than 130 rpm;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_3__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_3__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">45  <i>n</i>(0.2) g/kWh when <i>n</i> is 130 or more but less than 2,000 rpm;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_3__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_3__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">9.8 g/kWh when <i>n</i> is 2,000 rpm or more.</span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_4"><h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_4">Tier II</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_3" href="#chp_1__part_3">regulation 3</a> of this Annex, the operation of a marine diesel engine that is installed on a ship constructed on or after 1 January 2011 is prohibited, except when the emission of nitrogen oxides (calculated as the total weighted emission of NO2) from the engine is within the following limits, where <i>n</i> = rated engine speed (crankshaft revolutions per minute):</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_4__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_4__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">14.4 g/kWh when n is less than 130 rpm;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_4__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_4__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">44  <i>n</i>(0.23) g/kWh when <i>n</i> is 130 or more but less than 2,000 rpm;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_4__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_4__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">7.7 g/kWh when <i>n</i> is 2,000 rpm or more.</span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_5"><h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_5">Tier III</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51"><span class="akn-num">5.1.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_3" href="#chp_1__part_3">regulation 3</a> of this Annex, in an emission control area designated for Tier III NO<sub>x</sub> control under paragraph 6 of this regulation, the operation of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> that is <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__term_2">installed</span> on a ship:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">is prohibited except when the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__term_1">emission</span> of nitrogen oxides (calculated as the total weighted <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__term_2">emission</span> of NO<sub>x</sub>)<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__authorialNote_1"></a></sup> from the engine is within the following limits, where n = rated engine speed (crankshaft revolutions per minute):<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup></sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">"NO<sub>x</sub>" is corrected to "NO<sub>2</sub>" by Amendments to regulation 13 of MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__authorialNote_1__term_1">Annex</span> VI (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.271%2869%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.271%2869%29.pdf">MEPC.271(69)</a>); refer to Additional information</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__subpara_11" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__subpara_11"><span class="akn-num">1.1.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">3.4 g/kWh when n is less than 130 rpm;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__subpara_12" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__subpara_12"><span class="akn-num">1.2.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">9  <i>n</i>(0.2) g/kWh when <i>n</i> is 130 or more but less than 2,000 rpm;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__subpara_13" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_1__subpara_13"><span class="akn-num">1.3.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">2.0 g/kWh when <i>n</i> is 2,000 rpm or more;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-container" data-name="container" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__container_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__container_1"><span class="akn-p">when:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">that ship is constructed on or after 1 January 2016 and is operating in the North American <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_2__term_1">Emission</span> Control Area or the United States Caribbean Sea <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_2__term_2">Emission</span> Control Area;</span></span></span><span class="akn-container" data-name="container" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__container_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__container_2"><span class="akn-p">when:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">that ship is operating in an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_1">emission control area</span> designated for Tier III NO<sub>x</sub> control under paragraph 6 of this regulation, other than an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_2">emission control area</span> described in paragraph 5.1.2 of this regulation, and is constructed on or after the date of adoption of such an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_3">emission control area</span>, or a later date as may be specified in the amendment designating the NO<sub>x</sub> Tier III <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_51__subpara_3__term_4">emission control area</span>, whichever is later.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52"><span class="akn-num">5.2.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">The standards set forth in paragraph 5.1.1 of this regulation shall not apply to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1__term_2">installed</span> on a ship with a length (L), as defined in regulation 1.19 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_1__term_3">Annex</span> I to the present Convention, of less than 24 m when it has been specifically designed, and is used solely, for recreational purposes; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_2__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_2__term_2">installed</span> on a ship with a combined nameplate diesel engine propulsion power of less than 750 kW if it is demonstrated, to the satisfaction of the Administration, that the ship cannot comply with the standards set forth in paragraph 5.1.1 of this regulation because of design or construction limitations of the ship; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_2">installed</span> on a ship constructed prior to 1 January 2021 of less than 500 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_3">gross tonnage</span>, with a length (L), as defined in regulation 1.19 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_52__subpara_3__term_4">Annex</span> I to the present convention, of 24 m or over when it has been specifically designed, and is used solely, for recreational purposes.</span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_6"><h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_6"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_6__term_1">Emission control area</span></h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">For the purposes of this regulation, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6__term_1">emission</span> control areas shall be:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the North American area, which means the area described by the coordinates provided in appendix VII to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_1__term_1">Annex</span>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the United States Caribbean sea area, which means the area described by the coordinates provided in appendix VII to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_2__term_1">Annex</span>; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">any other sea area, including any port area, designated by the Organization in accordance with the criteria and procedures set forth in appendix III to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_6__subpara_3__term_1">Annex</span>.</span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_7" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_7"><h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_7" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_7">Marine diesel engines <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_7__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_7__term_1">installed</span> on a ship constructed prior to 1 January 2000</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_71" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_71"><span class="akn-num">7.1.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding paragraph 1.1.1 of this regulation, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_71__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_71__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> with a power output of more than 5,000 kW and a per cylinder displacement at or above 90 L <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_71__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_71__term_2">installed</span> on a ship constructed on or after 1 January 1990 but prior to 1 January 2000 shall comply with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_13__para_71__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_71__term_3">emission</span> limits set forth in paragraph 7.4 of this regulation, provided that an approved method[12] for that engine has been certified by an Administration of a Party and notification of such certification has been submitted to the Organization by the certifying Administration.[13] Compliance with this paragraph shall be demonstrated through one of the following:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_71__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_71__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">installation of the certified approved method, as confirmed by a survey using the verification procedure specified in the approved method file, including appropriate notation on the ships International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate of the presence of the approved method; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_71__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_71__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">certification of the engine confirming that it operates within the limits set forth in paragraph 3, 4, or 5.1.1 of this regulation and an appropriate notation of the engine certification on the ships International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_72" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_72"><span class="akn-num">7.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Paragraph 7.1 of this regulation shall apply no later than the first renewal survey that occurs 12 months or more after deposit of the notification in paragraph 7.1. If a shipowner of a ship on which an approved method is to be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_72__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_72__term_1">installed</span> can demonstrate to the satisfaction of the Administration that the approved method was not commercially available despite best efforts to obtain it, then that approved method shall be <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_72__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_72__term_2">installed</span> on the ship no later than the next annual survey of that ship that falls after the approved method is commercially available.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73"><span class="akn-num">7.3.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">With regard to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> with a power output of more than 5,000 kW and a per cylinder displacement at or above 90 L <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73__term_2">installed</span> on a ship constructed on or after 1 January 1990, but prior to 1 January 2000, the International Air Pollution Prevention Certificate shall, for a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73__term_3">marine diesel engine</span> to which paragraph 7.1 of this regulation applies, indicate one of the following:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">an approved method has been applied pursuant to paragraph 7.1.1 of this regulation;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the engine has been certified pursuant to paragraph 7.1.2 of this regulation;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">an approved method is not yet commercially available as described in paragraph 7.2 of this regulation; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_73__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">an approved method is not applicable.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_74" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_74"><span class="akn-num">7.4.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Subject to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_3" href="#chp_1__part_3">regulation 3</a> of this Annex, the operation of a marine diesel engine described in paragraph 7.1 of this regulation is prohibited, except when the emission of nitrogen oxides (calculated as the total weighted emission of NO2) from the engine is within the following limits, where n = rated engine speed (crankshaft revolutions per minute):</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_74__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_74__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">17.0 g/kWh when n is less than 130 rpm;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_74__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_74__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">45  n(0.2) g/kWh when n is 130 or more but less than 2,000 rpm; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_74__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_74__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">9.8 g/kWh when n is 2,000 rpm or more.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_75" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_75"><span class="akn-num">7.5.</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Certification of an approved method shall be in accordance with chapter 7 of the revised NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code 2008 and shall include verification:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">by the designer of the base <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Marine_diesel_engine" id="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_1__term_1">marine diesel engine</span> to which the approved method applies that the calculated effect of the approved method will not decrease engine rating by more than 1.0%, increase fuel consumption by more than 2.0% as measured according to the appropriate test cycle set forth in the revised NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code 2008, or adversely affect engine durability or reliability; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">that the cost of the approved method is not excessive, which is determined by a comparison of the amount of NO<sub>x</sub> reduced by the approved method to achieve the standard set forth in paragraph 7.4 of this regulation and the cost of purchasing and installing such approved method.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_2__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_2__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_2__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">The cost of an approved method shall not exceed 375 Special Drawing Rights/metric tonne NO<sub>x</sub> calculated in accordance with the cost-effectiveness (Ce) formula below:</span><span class="akn-p">Ce = [FORMULA]</span><span class="akn-p">Refer to Definitions for the cost-effectiveness formula in regulation 13.7.5 of the revised MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_2__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_75__subpara_2__authorialNote_1__term_1">Annex</span> VI (MEPC.1/Circ.678).</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_8" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_8"><h3 id="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_8" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__crossHeading_8">Certification</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_8" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_8"><span class="akn-num">8</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The revised NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code 2008 shall be applied in the certification, testing and measurement procedures for the standards set forth in this regulation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_13__para_9" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_9"><span class="akn-num">9</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The procedures for determining NO<sub>x</sub> emissions set out in the revised NO<sub>x</sub> Technical Code 2008 are intended to be representative of the normal operation of the engine. Defeat devices and irrational <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_13__para_9__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_13__para_9__term_1">emission</span> control strategies undermine this intention and shall not be allowed. This regulation shall not prevent the use of auxiliary control devices that are used to protect the engine and/or its ancillary equipment against operating conditions that could result in damage or failure or that are used to facilitate the starting of the engine.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_14" data-eId="chp_3__part_14"><h2>Regulation 14  Sulphur oxides (SOx) and particulate matter</h2>
<div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_1"><h3 id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_1">General requirements</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">The sulphur content of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_1__term_1">fuel oil</span> used on board ships shall not exceed the following limits:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_1__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_1__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">4.50% m/m prior to 1 January 2012;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The worldwide average sulphur content of residual <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_2__term_1">fuel oil</span> supplied for use on board ships shall be monitored taking into account guidelines developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_14__para_2__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_14__para_2__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_2__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2010 Guidelines for monitoring the worldwide average sulphur content of fuel oils supplied for use on board ships (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.192%2861%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.192%2861%29.pdf">MEPC.192(61)</a>, as amended by resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.273%2869%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.273%2869%29.pdf">MEPC.273(69)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_2"><h3 id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_2">Requirements within <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_2__term_1">emission</span> control areas</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">For the purpose of this regulation, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__term_1">emission</span> control areas shall include:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the Baltic Sea area as defined in regulation 1.11.2 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_1__term_1">Annex</span> I and the North Sea as defined in regulation 1.14.6 of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_1__term_2">Annex</span> V;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the North American area as described by the coordinates provided in appendix VII to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_2__term_1">Annex</span>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the United States Caribbean Sea area as described by the coordinates provided in appendix VII to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_3__term_1">Annex</span>; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">any other sea area, including any port area, designated by the Organization in accordance with the criteria and procedures set forth in appendix III to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_3__subpara_4__term_1">Annex</span>.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">While ships are operating within an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4__term_1">emission control area</span>, the sulphur content of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4__term_2">fuel oil</span> used on board ships shall not exceed the following limits:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">1.50% m/m prior to 1 July 2010;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">1.00% m/m on and after 1 July 2010; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">0.10% m/m on and after 1 January 2015.</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Prior to 1 January 2020, the sulphur content of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_4__subpara_4__term_1">fuel oil</span> referred to in paragraph 4 of this regulation shall not apply to ships operating in the North American area or the United States Caribbean Sea area defined in paragraph 3, built on or before 1 August 2011 that are powered by propulsion boilers that were not originally designed for continued operation on marine distillate fuel or natural gas.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The sulphur content of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_5__term_1">fuel oil</span> referred to in paragraph 1 and paragraph 4 of this regulation shall be documented by its supplier as required by <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_18" href="#chp_3__part_18">regulation 18</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Those ships using separate fuel oils to comply with paragraph 4 of this regulation and entering or leaving an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_1">emission control area</span> set forth in paragraph 3 of this regulation shall carry a written procedure showing how the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_2">fuel oil</span> changeover is to be done, allowing sufficient time for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_3">fuel oil</span> service system to be fully flushed of all fuel oils exceeding the applicable sulphur content specified in paragraph 4 of this regulation prior to entry into an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_4">emission control area</span>. The volume of low sulphur fuel oils in each tank as well as the date, time and position of the ship when any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_5">fuel oil</span> changeover operation is completed prior to the entry into an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_6__term_6">emission control area</span> or commenced after exit from such an area shall be recorded in such logbook as prescribed by the Administration.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_7" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_7"><span class="akn-num">7</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">During the first 12 months immediately following entry into force of an amendment designating a specific <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_14__para_7__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_7__term_1">emission control area</span> under paragraph 3 of this regulation, ships operating in that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission_control_area" id="chp_3__part_14__para_7__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_7__term_2">emission control area</span> are exempt from the requirements in paragraphs 4 and 6 of this regulation and from the requirements of paragraph 5 of this regulation insofar as they relate to paragraph 4 of this regulation.</span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3">
<h3 id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3">Review provision<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1"></a></sup>
</h3>
<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup></sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Effective date of implementation of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1__term_1">fuel oil</span> standard in regulation 14.1.3 of MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__crossHeading_3__authorialNote_1__term_2">Annex</span> VI (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.280%2870%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.280%2870%29.pdf">MEPC.280(70)</a>).</span></span></span>
</div>
