<span class="akn-container" data-name="container" id="chp_3__part_14__container_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__container_1"></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8"><span class="akn-num">8</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">A review of the standard set forth in paragraph 1.3 of this regulation shall be completed by 2018 to determine the availability of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8__term_1">fuel oil</span> to comply with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8__term_2">fuel oil</span> standard set forth in that paragraph and shall take into account the following elements:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the global market supply and demand for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_1__term_1">fuel oil</span> to comply with paragraph 1.3 of this regulation that exist at the time that the review is conducted;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">an analysis of the trends in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_2__term_1">fuel oil</span> markets; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_8__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">any other relevant issue.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_9" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_9"><span class="akn-num">9</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Organization shall establish a group of experts, comprising representatives with the appropriate expertise in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_14__para_9__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_9__term_1">fuel oil</span> market and appropriate maritime, environmental, scientific and legal expertise, to conduct the review referred to in paragraph 8 of this regulation. The group of experts shall develop the appropriate information to inform the decision to be taken by the Parties.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_14__para_10" data-eId="chp_3__part_14__para_10"><span class="akn-num">10</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Parties, based on the information developed by the group of experts, may decide whether it is possible for ships to comply with the date in paragraph 1.3 of this regulation. If a decision is taken that it is not possible for ships to comply, then the standard in that paragraph shall become effective on 1 January 2025.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_15" data-eId="chp_3__part_15"><h2>Regulation 15  Volatile organic compounds (VOCs)</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the emissions of VOCs from a tanker are to be regulated in a port or ports or a terminal or terminals under the jurisdiction of a Party, they shall be regulated in accordance with the provisions of this regulation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A Party regulating tankers for VOC emissions shall submit a notification to the Organization.[17] This notification shall include information on the size of tankers to be controlled, the cargoes requiring vapour <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_15__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_2__term_1">emission</span> control systems and the effective date of such control. The notification shall be submitted at least six months before the effective date.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A Party that designates ports or terminals at which VOC emissions from tankers are to be regulated shall ensure that vapour <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_15__para_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_3__term_1">emission</span> control systems, approved by that Party taking into account the safety standards for such systems developed by the Organization,[18] are provided in any designated port and terminal and are operated safely and in a manner so as to avoid undue delay to a ship.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Organization shall circulate a list of the ports and terminals designated by Parties to other Parties and Member States of the Organization for their information.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A tanker to which paragraph 1 of this regulation applies shall be provided with a vapour <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_15__para_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_5__term_1">emission</span> collection system approved by the Administration taking into account the safety standards for such systems developed by the Organization, and shall use this system during the loading of relevant cargoes. A port or terminal that has <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_15__para_5__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_5__term_2">installed</span> vapour <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_15__para_5__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_5__term_3">emission</span> control systems in accordance with this regulation may accept tankers that are not fitted with vapour collection systems for a period of three years after the effective date identified in paragraph 2 of this regulation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">A tanker carrying crude oil shall have on board and implement a VOC management plan approved by the Administration.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_15__para_6__authorialNote_1"></a></sup> Such a plan shall be prepared taking into account the guidelines developed by the Organization. The plan shall be specific to each ship and shall at least:<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_15__para_6__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_6__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup></sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Guidelines for the development of a VOC management plan (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.185%2859%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.185%2859%29.pdf">MEPC.185(59)</a>). Refer also to Technical information on systems and operation to assist development of VOC management plans (MEPC.1/Circ.680), and Technical information on a vapour pressure control system to facilitate the development and update of VOC management plans (MEPC.1/Circ.719).</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">provide written procedures for minimizing VOC emissions during the loading, sea passage and discharge of cargo;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">give consideration to the additional VOC generated by crude oil washing;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">identify a person responsible for implementing the plan; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_6__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for ships on international voyages, be written in the working language of the master and officers and, if the working language of the master and officers is not English, French or Spanish, include a translation into one of these languages.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_15__para_7" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_7"><span class="akn-num">7</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This regulation shall also apply to gas carriers only if the types of loading and containment systems allow safe retention of non-methane VOCs on board or their safe return ashore.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_15__para_7__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_15__para_7__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_15__para_7__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to the International Code for the construction and equipment of ships carrying liquefied gases in bulk (resolution MSC.370(93)).</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_16" data-eId="chp_3__part_16"><h2>Regulation 16  <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incineration" id="chp_3__part_16__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__term_1">Shipboard incineration</span>
</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except as provided in paragraph 4 of this regulation, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incineration" id="chp_3__part_16__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_1__term_1">shipboard incineration</span> shall be allowed only in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incinerator" id="chp_3__part_16__para_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_1__term_2">shipboard incinerator</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incineration" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__term_1">Shipboard incineration</span> of the following substances shall be prohibited:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">residues of cargoes subject to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_1__term_1">Annex</span> I, II or III or related contaminated packing materials;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">polychlorinated biphenyls (PCBs);</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">garbage, as defined by <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_3__term_1">Annex</span> V, containing more than traces of heavy metals;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">refined petroleum products containing halogen compounds;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_5"><span class="akn-num">.5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">sewage sludge and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Sludge_oil" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_5__term_1">sludge oil</span> either of which is not generated on board the ship; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_2__subpara_6"><span class="akn-num">.6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">exhaust gas cleaning system residues.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incineration" id="chp_3__part_16__para_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_3__term_1">Shipboard incineration</span> of polyvinyl chlorides (PVCs) shall be prohibited, except in shipboard incinerators for which IMO Type Approval Certificates[20] have been issued.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Shipboard_incineration" id="chp_3__part_16__para_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_4__term_1">Shipboard incineration</span> of sewage sludge and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Sludge_oil" id="chp_3__part_16__para_4__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_4__term_2">sludge oil</span> generated during normal operation of a ship may also take place in the main or auxiliary power plant or boilers, but in those cases, shall not take place inside ports, harbours and estuaries.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Nothing in this regulation neither:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_5__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_5__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">affects the prohibition in, or other requirements of, the Convention on the Prevention of Marine Pollution by Dumping of Wastes and Other Matter, 1972, as amended, and the 1996 Protocol thereto, nor</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_5__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_5__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">precludes the development, installation and operation of alternative design shipboard thermal waste treatment devices that meet or exceed the requirements of this regulation.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_61" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_61"><span class="akn-num">6.1.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except as provided in paragraph 6.2 of this regulation, each incinerator on a ship constructed on or after 1 January 2000 or incinerator that is <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_16__para_61__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_61__term_1">installed</span> on board a ship on or after 1 January 2000 shall meet the requirements contained in appendix IV to this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_16__para_61__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_61__term_2">Annex</span>. Each incinerator subject to this paragraph shall be approved by the Administration taking into account the standard specification for shipboard incinerators developed by the Organization;<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_16__para_61__authorialNote_1"></a></sup> or<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_16__para_61__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_61__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup></sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2014 Standard specification for shipboard incinerators (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.244%2866%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.244%2866%29.pdf">MEPC.244(66)</a>), or Standard specification for shipboard incinerators (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.76%2840%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.76%2840%29.pdf">MEPC.76(40)</a>, as amended by resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.93%2845%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.93%2845%29.pdf">MEPC.93(45)</a>), and Type approval of shipboard incinerators (MEPC.1/Circ.793).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_62" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_62"><span class="akn-num">6.2.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration may allow exclusion from the application of paragraph 6.1 of this regulation to any incinerator <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_16__para_62__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_62__term_1">installed</span> on board a ship before 19 May 2005, provided that the ship is solely engaged in voyages within waters subject to the sovereignty or jurisdiction of the State the flag of which the ship is entitled to fly.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_7" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_7"><span class="akn-num">7</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Incinerators <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_16__para_7__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_7__term_1">installed</span> in accordance with the requirements of paragraph 6.1 of this regulation shall be provided with a manufacturers operating manual, which is to be retained with the unit and which shall specify how to operate the incinerator within the limits described in paragraph 2 of appendix IV of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_16__para_7__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_7__term_2">Annex</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_8" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_8"><span class="akn-num">8</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Personnel responsible for the operation of an incinerator <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_16__para_8__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_8__term_1">installed</span> in accordance with the requirements of paragraph 6.1 of this regulation shall be trained to implement the guidance provided in the manufacturers operating manual as required by paragraph 7 of this regulation.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_16__para_9" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_9"><span class="akn-num">9</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For incinerators <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_3__part_16__para_9__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_16__para_9__term_1">installed</span> in accordance with the requirements of paragraph 6.1 of this regulation the combustion chamber gas outlet temperature shall be monitored at all times the unit is in operation. Where that incinerator is of the continuous-feed type, waste shall not be fed into the unit when the combustion chamber gas outlet temperature is below 850C. Where that incinerator is of the batch-loaded type, the unit shall be designed so that the combustion chamber gas outlet temperature shall reach 600C within five minutes after start-up and will thereafter stabilize at a temperature not less than 850C.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_17" data-eId="chp_3__part_17"><h2>Regulation 17  Reception facilities</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Each Party undertakes to ensure the provision of facilities adequate to meet the:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">needs of ships using its repair ports for the reception of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_1__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span> and equipment containing such substances when removed from ships;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">needs of ships using its ports, terminals or repair ports for the reception of exhaust gas cleaning residues from an exhaust gas cleaning system;</span></span></span><span class="akn-container" data-name="container" id="chp_3__part_17__para_1__container_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_1__container_1"><span class="akn-p">without causing undue delay to ships, and</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">needs in ship-breaking facilities for the reception of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Ozone_depleting_substances" id="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_1__subpara_3__term_1">ozone-depleting substances</span> and equipment containing such substances when removed from ships.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Small Island Developing States<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup> may satisfy the requirements in paragraph 1 of this regulation through regional arrangements when, because of those States unique circumstances, such arrangements are the only practical means to satisfy these requirements. Parties participating in a regional arrangement shall develop a Regional Reception Facilities Plan, taking into account the guidelines developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_2"></a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2012 Guidelines for the development of a regional reception facilities plan (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.221%2863%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.221%2863%29.pdf">MEPC.221(63)</a>).</span></span></span><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_2"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup></sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2011 Guidelines for reception facilities under MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_2__authorialNote_2__term_1">Annex</span> VI (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.199%2862%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.199%2862%29.pdf">MEPC.199(62)</a>).</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p">The Government of each Party participating in the arrangement shall consult with the Organization for circulation to the Parties of the present Convention:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_2__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_2__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">how the Regional Reception Facilities Plan takes into account the Guidelines;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_2__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_2__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">particulars of the identified Regional Ships Waste Reception Centres; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_2__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_2__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">particulars of those ports with only limited facilities.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a particular port or terminal of a Party is, taking into account the guidelines to be developed by the Organization, remotely located from, or lacking in, the industrial infrastructure necessary to manage and process those substances referred to in paragraph 1 of this regulation and therefore cannot accept such substances, then the Party shall inform the Organization of any such port or terminal so that this information may be circulated to all Parties and Member States of the Organization for their information and any appropriate action. Each Party that has provided the Organization with such information shall also notify the Organization of its ports and terminals where reception facilities are available to manage and process such substances.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_17__para_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_17__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each Party shall notify the Organization for transmission to the Members of the Organization of all cases where the facilities provided under this regulation are unavailable or alleged to be inadequate.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_18" data-eId="chp_3__part_18"><h2>Regulation 18  <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__term_1">Fuel oil</span> availability and quality</h2>
<div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_1"><h3 id="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_1">
<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_1__term_1">Fuel oil</span> availability</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each Party shall take all reasonable steps to promote the availability of fuel oils that comply with this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_18__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_1__term_1">Annex</span> and inform the Organization of the availability of compliant fuel oils in its ports and terminals.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21"><span class="akn-num">2.1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">If a ship is found by a Party not to be in compliance with the standards for compliant fuel oils set forth in this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21__term_1">Annex</span>, the competent authority of the Party is entitled to require the ship to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">present a record of the actions taken to attempt to achieve compliance; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">provide evidence that it attempted to purchase compliant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_1">fuel oil</span> in accordance with its voyage plan and, if it was not made available where planned, that attempts were made to locate alternative sources for such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_2">fuel oil</span> and that despite best efforts to obtain compliant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_3">fuel oil</span>, no such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_21__subpara_2__term_4">fuel oil</span> was made available for purchase.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_22" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_22"><span class="akn-num">2.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The ship should not be required to deviate from its intended voyage or to delay unduly the voyage in order to achieve compliance.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_23" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_23"><span class="akn-num">2.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a ship provides the information set forth in paragraph 2.1 of this regulation, a Party shall take into account all relevant circumstances and the evidence presented to determine the appropriate action to take, including not taking control measures.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_24" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_24"><span class="akn-num">2.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A ship shall notify its Administration and the competent authority of the relevant port of destination when it cannot purchase compliant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_24__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_24__term_1">fuel oil</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_25" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_25"><span class="akn-num">2.5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A Party shall notify the Organization when a ship has presented evidence of the non-availability of compliant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_25__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_25__term_1">fuel oil</span>.</span></span></span><div class="akn-crossHeading" id="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_2"><h3 id="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_2">
<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__crossHeading_2__term_1">Fuel oil</span> quality</h3></div>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__term_1">Fuel oil</span> for combustion purposes delivered to and used on board ships to which this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__term_2">Annex</span> applies shall meet the following requirements:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">except as provided in paragraph 3.2 of this regulation:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_11" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_11"><span class="akn-num">1.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_11__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_11__term_1">fuel oil</span> shall be blends of hydrocarbons derived from petroleum refining. This shall not preclude the incorporation of small amounts of additives intended to improve some aspects of performance;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_12" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_12"><span class="akn-num">1.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_12__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_12__term_1">fuel oil</span> shall be free from inorganic acid; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13"><span class="akn-num">1.3</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__term_1">fuel oil</span> shall not include any added substance or chemical waste that:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__subpara_131" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__subpara_131"><span class="akn-num">1.3.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">jeopardizes the safety of ships or adversely affects the performance of the machinery, or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__subpara_132" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__subpara_132"><span class="akn-num">1.3.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">is harmful to personnel, or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__subpara_133" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_1__subpara_13__subpara_133"><span class="akn-num">1.3.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">contributes overall to additional air pollution.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__term_1">fuel oil</span> for combustion purposes derived by methods other than petroleum refining shall not:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_21" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_21"><span class="akn-num">2.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">exceed the applicable sulphur content set forth in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_14" href="#chp_3__part_14">regulation 14</a> of this Annex;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_22" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_22"><span class="akn-num">2.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">cause an engine to exceed the applicable NO<sub>x</sub> <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Emission" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_22__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_22__term_1">emission</span> limit set forth in paragraphs 3, 4, 5.1.1 and 7.4 of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_13" href="#chp_3__part_13">regulation 13</a>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23"><span class="akn-num">2.3</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">contain inorganic acid; or</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23__subpara_241" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23__subpara_241"><span class="akn-num">2.4.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">jeopardize the safety of ships or adversely affect the performance of the machinery, or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23__subpara_242" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23__subpara_242"><span class="akn-num">2.4.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">be harmful to personnel, or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23__subpara_243" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_3__subpara_2__subpara_23__subpara_243"><span class="akn-num">2.4.3.</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">contribute overall to additional air pollution.</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This regulation does not apply to coal in its solid form or nuclear fuels. Paragraphs 5, 6, 7.1, 7.2, 8.1, 8.2, 9.2, 9.3, and 9.4 of this regulation do not apply to gas fuels such as liquefied natural gas, compressed natural gas or liquefied petroleum gas. The sulphur content of gas fuels delivered to a ship specifically for combustion purposes on board that ship shall be documented by the supplier.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For each ship subject to regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_6" href="#chp_2__part_6">6</a> of this Annex, details of fuel oil for combustion purposes delivered to and used on board shall be recorded by means of a bunker delivery note that shall contain at least the information specified in appendix V to this Annex.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The bunker delivery note shall be kept on board the ship in such a place as to be readily available for inspection at all reasonable times. It shall be retained for a period of three years after the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_6__term_1">fuel oil</span> has been delivered on board.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_71" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_71"><span class="akn-num">7.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The competent authority of a Party may inspect the bunker delivery notes on board any ship to which this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_18__para_71__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_71__term_1">Annex</span> applies while the ship is in its port or offshore terminal, may make a copy of each delivery note, and may require the master or person in charge of the ship to certify that each copy is a true copy of such bunker delivery note. The competent authority may also verify the contents of each note through consultations with the port where the note was issued.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_72" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_72"><span class="akn-num">7.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The inspection of the bunker delivery notes and the taking of certified copies by the competent authority under paragraph 7.1 shall be performed as expeditiously as possible without causing the ship to be unduly delayed.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_81" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_81"><span class="akn-num">8.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The bunker delivery note shall be accompanied by a representative sample of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_81__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_81__term_1">fuel oil</span> delivered taking into account guidelines developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_3__part_18__para_81__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup> The sample is to be sealed and signed by the suppliers representative and the master or officer in charge of the bunker operation on completion of bunkering operations and retained under the ships control until the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_81__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_81__term_2">fuel oil</span> is substantially consumed, but in any case for a period of not less than 12 months from the time of delivery.<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_3__part_18__para_81__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_81__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2009 Guidelines for the sampling of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_81__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_81__authorialNote_1__term_1">fuel oil</span> for determination of compliance with the revised MARPOL <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_18__para_81__authorialNote_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_81__authorialNote_1__term_2">Annex</span> VI (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.182%2859%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.182%2859%29.pdf">MEPC.182(59)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_82" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_82"><span class="akn-num">8.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an Administration requires the representative sample to be analysed, it shall be done in accordance with the verification procedure set forth in appendix VI to determine whether the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_82__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_82__term_1">fuel oil</span> meets the requirements of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_3__part_18__para_82__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_82__term_2">Annex</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9"><span class="akn-num">9</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">Parties undertake to ensure that appropriate authorities designated by them:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">maintain a register of local suppliers of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_1__term_1">fuel oil</span>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">require local suppliers to provide the bunker delivery note and sample as required by this regulation, certified by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_2__term_1">fuel oil</span> supplier that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_2__term_2">fuel oil</span> meets the requirements of regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_14" href="#chp_3__part_14">14</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_18" href="#chp_3__part_18">18</a> of this Annex;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">require local suppliers to retain a copy of the bunker delivery note for at least three years for inspection and verification by the port State as necessary;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">take action as appropriate against <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_4__term_1">fuel oil</span> suppliers that have been found to deliver <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_4__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_4__term_2">fuel oil</span> that does not comply with that stated on the bunker delivery note;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_5" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_5"><span class="akn-num">.5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">inform the Administration of any ship receiving <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_5__term_1">fuel oil</span> found to be non-compliant with the requirements of regulation <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_14" href="#chp_3__part_14">14</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_18" href="#chp_3__part_18">18</a> of this Annex; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_6" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_6"><span class="akn-num">.6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">inform the Organization for transmission to Parties and Member States of the Organization of all cases where <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_6__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_9__subpara_6__term_1">fuel oil</span> suppliers have failed to meet the requirements specified in regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_14" href="#chp_3__part_14">14</a> or <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_18" href="#chp_3__part_18">18</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_10" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_10"><span class="akn-num">10</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">In connection with port State inspections carried out by Parties, the Parties further undertake to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">inform the Party or non-Party under whose jurisdiction a bunker delivery note was issued of cases of delivery of non-compliant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_1__term_1">fuel oil</span>, giving all relevant information; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">ensure that remedial action as appropriate is taken to bring non-compliant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Fuel_oil" id="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_10__subpara_2__term_1">fuel oil</span> discovered into compliance.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_3__part_18__para_11" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_11"><span class="akn-num">11</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For every ship of 400 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_3__part_18__para_11__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_18__para_11__term_1">gross tonnage</span> and above on scheduled services with frequent and regular port calls, an Administration may decide after application and consultation with affected States that compliance with paragraph 6 of this regulation may be documented in an alternative manner that gives similar certainty of compliance with regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_14" href="#chp_3__part_14">14</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_3__part_18" href="#chp_3__part_18">18</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_4" data-eId="chp_4"><h2>Chapter 4<br>Regulations on energy efficiency for ships</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_19" data-eId="chp_4__part_19"><h2>Regulation 19  Application</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This chapter shall apply to all ships of 400 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_4__part_19__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_1__term_1">gross tonnage</span> and above.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of this chapter shall not apply to:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_2__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_2__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">ships solely engaged in voyages within waters subject to the sovereignty or jurisdiction of the State the flag of which the ship is entitled to fly. However, each Party should ensure, by the adoption of appropriate measures, that such ships are constructed and act in a manner consistent with the requirements of chapter 4 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_4__part_19__para_2__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_2__subpara_1__term_1">Annex</span>, so far as is reasonable and practicable.</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_2__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_2__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">ships not propelled by mechanical means, and platforms including FPSOs and FSUs and drilling rigs, regardless of their propulsion.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_3" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_20" href="#chp_4__part_20">20</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">21</a> of this Annex shall not apply to ships which have non-conventional propulsion, except that regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_20" href="#chp_4__part_20">20</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">21</a> shall apply to cruise passenger ships having non-conventional propulsion and LNG carriers having conventional or non-conventional propulsion, delivered on or after 1 September 2019, as defined in paragraph 43 of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">regulation 2</a>. Regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_20" href="#chp_4__part_20">20</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">21</a> shall not apply to cargo ships having ice-breaking capability.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_4" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph 1 of this regulation, the Administration may waive the requirement for a ship of 400 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_4__part_19__para_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_4__term_1">gross tonnage</span> and above from complying with regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_20" href="#chp_4__part_20">20</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_21" href="#chp_4__part_21">21</a> of this Annex.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">The provision of paragraph 4 of this regulation shall not apply to ships of 400 <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Gross_tonnage" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__term_1">gross tonnage</span> and above:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">for which the building contract is placed on or after 1 January 2017; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">in the absence of a building contract, the keel of which is laid or which is at <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-A_similar_stage_of_construction" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_2__term_1">a similar stage of construction</span> on or after 1 July 2017; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">the delivery of which is on or after 1 July 2019; or</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_4" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_4"><span class="akn-num">.4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">in cases of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_4__term_1">major conversion</span> of a new or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship" id="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_4__term_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_5__subpara_4__term_2">existing ship</span>, as defined in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">regulation 2</a>.24 of this Annex, on or after 1 January 2017, and in which regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a>.4.2 and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_2__part_5" href="#chp_2__part_5">5</a>.4.3 of this Annex apply.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_19__para_6" data-eId="chp_4__part_19__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration of a Party to the present Convention which allows application of paragraph 4, or suspends, withdraws or declines the application of that paragraph, to a ship entitled to fly its flag shall forthwith communicate to the Organization for circulation to the Parties to the present Protocol particulars thereof, for their information.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_20" data-eId="chp_4__part_20"><h2>Regulation 20  Attained Energy Efficiency Design Index (attained EEDI)</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">The attained EEDI shall be calculated for:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_1__term_1">new ship</span>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_2__term_1">new ship</span> which has undergone a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_2__term_2">major conversion</span>; and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">each new or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3__term_1">existing ship</span> which has undergone a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3__term_2">major conversion</span>, that is so extensive that the ship is regarded by the Administration as a newly-constructed ship, which falls into one or more of the categories in regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.25 to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.35, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.38 and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.39 of this Annex. The attained EEDI shall be specific to each ship and shall indicate the estimated performance of the ship in terms of energy efficiency, and be accompanied by the EEDI technical file that contains the information necessary for the calculation of the attained EEDI and that shows the process of calculation. The attained EEDI shall be verified, based on the EEDI technical file, either by the Administration or by any organization duly authorized by it.<sup><a href="#chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_1__subpara_3__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Guidelines for the authorization of organizations acting on behalf of the Administration (resolution A.739(18), as amended by resolution MSC.208(81)), and Specifications on the survey and certification functions of recognized organizations acting on behalf of the Administration (resolution A.789(19), as may be amended).</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_20__para_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The attained EEDI shall be calculated taking into account guidelines<sup><a href="#chp_4__part_20__para_2__authorialNote_1"></a></sup> developed by the Organization.<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_4__part_20__para_2__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_20__para_2__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup></sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2014 Guidelines on the method of calculation of the Energy Efficiency Design Index for new ships (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.245%2866%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.245%2866%29.pdf">MEPC.245(66)</a>, as amended by resolutions <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.263%2868%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.263%2868%29.pdf">MEPC.263(68)</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.281%2870%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.281%2870%29.pdf">MEPC.281(70)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_21" data-eId="chp_4__part_21"><h2>Regulation 21  Required EEDI</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p">For each:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_1__term_1">new ship</span>,</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-New_ship" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_2__term_1">new ship</span> which has undergone a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_2__term_2">major conversion</span>, and</span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_3" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_3"><span class="akn-num">.3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">new or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_3__term_1">existing ship</span> which has undergone a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_3__term_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_1__subpara_3__term_2">major conversion</span> that is so extensive that the ship is regarded by the Administration as a newly-constructed ship, which falls into one of the categories in regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.25 to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.31, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.33 to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.35, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.38 and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">2</a>.39 and to which this chapter is applicable, the attained EEDI shall be as follows:</span><span class="akn-p">[FORMULA]</span><span class="akn-p">where X is the reduction factor specified in table 1 for the required EEDI compared to the EEDI reference line.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For each new and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Existing_ship" id="chp_4__part_21__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_2__term_1">existing ship</span> that has undergone a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Major_conversion" id="chp_4__part_21__para_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_2__term_2">major conversion</span> which is so extensive that the ship is regarded by the Administration as a newly constructed ship, the attained EEDI shall be calculated and meet the requirement of paragraph 21.1 with the reduction factor applicable corresponding to the ship type and size of the converted ship at the date of the contract of the conversion, <span class="akn-p">* Reduction factor to be linearly interpolated between the two values dependent upon vessel size. The lower value of the reduction factor is to be applied to the smaller ship size.</span><span class="akn-p">** Phase 1 commences for those ships on 1 September 2015.</span><span class="akn-p">*** Reduction factor applies to those ships delivered on or after 1 September 2019, as defined in paragraph 43 of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_1__part_2" href="#chp_1__part_2">regulation 2</a>.</span><span class="akn-p">Note: n/a means that no required EEDI applies.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_3" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The reference line values shall be calculated as follows:</span><span class="akn-p">Reference line value = <i>a  bc</i></span><span class="akn-p">where <i>a</i>, <i>b</i> and <i>c</i> are the parameters given in table 2.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_4" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the design of a ship allows it to fall into more than one of the above ship type definitions specified in table 2, the required EEDI for the ship shall be the most stringent (the lowest) required EEDI.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_5" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_5"><span class="akn-num">5</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For each ship to which this regulation applies, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Installed" id="chp_4__part_21__para_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_5__term_1">installed</span> propulsion power shall not be less than the propulsion power needed to maintain the manoeuvrability of the ship under adverse conditions as defined in the guidelines to be developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_4__part_21__para_5__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_4__part_21__para_5__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_5__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2013 Interim Guidelines for determining minimum propulsion power to maintain the manoeuvrability of ships in adverse conditions (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.232%2865%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.232%2865%29.pdf">MEPC.232(65)</a>, as amended by resolutions <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.255%2867%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.255%2867%29.pdf">MEPC.255(67)</a> and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.262%2868%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.262%2868%29.pdf">MEPC.262(68)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_21__para_6" data-eId="chp_4__part_21__para_6"><span class="akn-num">6</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">At the beginning of phase 1 and at the midpoint of phase 2, the Organization shall review the status of technological developments and, if proven necessary, amend the time periods, the EEDI reference line parameters for relevant ship types and reduction rates set out in this regulation.</span><span class="akn-p">Table 2 - Parameters for determination of reference values for the different ship types</span><div
