</table></div></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_22" data-eId="chp_4__part_22"><h2>Regulation 22  Ship Energy Efficiency Management Plan (SEEMP)</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_22__para_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_22__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each ship shall keep on board a ship specific Ship Energy Efficiency Management Plan (SEEMP). This may form part of the ships Safety Management System (SMS).</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_22__para_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_22__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The SEEMP shall be developed taking into account guidelines adopted by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_4__part_22__para_2__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_4__part_22__para_2__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_22__para_2__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to 2016 Guidelines for the development of a Ship Energy Efficiency Management Plan (SEEMP) (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.282%2870%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.282%2870%29.pdf">MEPC.282(70)</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_4__part_23" data-eId="chp_4__part_23"><h2>Regulation 23  Promotion of technical cooperation and transfer of technology relating to the improvement of energy efficiency of ships<sup><a href="#chp_4__part_23__authorialNote_1"></a></sup>
</h2>
<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_4__part_23__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_23__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup></sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Promotion of technical cooperation and transfer of technology relating to the improvement of energy efficiency of ships (resolution <a class="akn-ref" data-href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.229%2865%29.pdf" href="http://www.imo.org/en/KnowledgeCentre/IndexofIMOResolutions/Marine-Environment-Protection-Committee-%28MEPC%29/Documents/MEPC.229%2865%29.pdf">MEPC.229(65)</a>), and Model agreement between governments on technological cooperation for the implementation of the regulations in chapter 4 of MARPOL Annex VI (MEPC.1/Circ.861).</span></span></span><span class="akn-intro"></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_23__para_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_23__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Administrations shall, in cooperation with the Organization and other international bodies, promote and provide, as appropriate, support directly or through the Organization to States, especially developing States, that request technical assistance.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_4__part_23__para_2" data-eId="chp_4__part_23__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Administration of a Party shall cooperate actively with other Parties, subject to its national laws, regulations and policies, to promote the development and transfer of technology and exchange of information to States which request technical assistance, particularly developing States, in respect of the implementation of measures to fulfil the requirements of chapter 4 of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_4__part_23__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_4__part_23__para_2__term_1">Annex</span>, in particular regulations <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_19" href="#chp_4__part_19">19</a>.4 to <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#chp_4__part_19" href="#chp_4__part_19">19</a>.6.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_5" data-eId="chp_5"><h2>Chapter 5<br>Verification of compliance with the provisions of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_5__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__term_1">Annex</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_5__part_24" data-eId="chp_5__part_24"><h2>Regulation 24  Application</h2>
<span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Parties shall use the provisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Code_for_Implementation" id="chp_5__part_24__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_24__term_1">Code for Implementation</span> in the execution of their obligations and responsibilities contained in this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_5__part_24__term_2" data-eId="chp_5__part_24__term_2">Annex</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_5__part_25" data-eId="chp_5__part_25"><h2>Regulation 25  Verification of compliance</h2>
<span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_5__part_25__para_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_1"><span class="akn-num">1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every Party shall be subject to periodic audits by the Organization in accordance with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Standard" id="chp_5__part_25__para_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_1__term_1">audit standard</span> to verify compliance with and implementation of this <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Annex" id="chp_5__part_25__para_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_1__term_2">Annex</span>.</span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_5__part_25__para_2" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_2"><span class="akn-num">2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The Secretary-General of the Organization shall have responsibility for administering the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Scheme" id="chp_5__part_25__para_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_2__term_1">Audit Scheme</span>, based on the guidelines developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_5__part_25__para_2__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_5__part_25__para_2__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_2__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Framework and Procedures for the IMO Member State <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Scheme" id="chp_5__part_25__para_2__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_2__authorialNote_1__term_1">Audit Scheme</span> (resolution A.1067(28)).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_5__part_25__para_3" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_3"><span class="akn-num">3</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every Party shall have responsibility for facilitating the conduct of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit" id="chp_5__part_25__para_3__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_3__term_1">audit</span> and implementation of a programme of actions to address the findings, based on the guidelines developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_5__part_25__para_3__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_5__part_25__para_3__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_3__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Framework and Procedures for the IMO Member State <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Scheme" id="chp_5__part_25__para_3__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_3__authorialNote_1__term_1">Audit Scheme</span> (resolution A.1067(28)).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-paragraph" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4"><span class="akn-num">4</span><span class="akn-intro"><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4__term_1">Audit</span> of all Parties shall be:</span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_1"><span class="akn-num">.1</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">based on an overall schedule developed by the Secretary-General of the Organization, taking into account the guidelines developed by the Organization;<sup><a href="#chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_1__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup> and<span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_1__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_1__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Framework and Procedures for the IMO Member State <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Scheme" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_1__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_1__authorialNote_1__term_1">Audit Scheme</span> (resolution A.1067(28)).</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-subparagraph" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_2" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_2"><span class="akn-num">.2</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">conducted at periodic intervals, taking into account the guidelines developed by the Organization.<sup><a href="#chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_2__authorialNote_1">*</a></sup><span class="akn-authorialNote" data-marker="*" data-placement="bottom" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_2__authorialNote_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_2__authorialNote_1"><span class="akn-authorialNote--marker"><sup>*</sup></span><span class="akn-authorialNote--content"><span class="akn-p">Refer to Framework and Procedures for the IMO Member State <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-Audit_Scheme" id="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_2__authorialNote_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_5__part_25__para_4__subpara_2__authorialNote_1__term_1">Audit Scheme</span> (resolution A.1067(28)).</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section></section></span></article></span>
